< Review>
I feel differently about Thrive now. I went to two locations after the first bad experience. This location in Santee with Dr. Jungman was a good experience. I had called various Thrives to see which had the soonest appointment and ended up here. I researched as much as possible before calling why my puppy was sick. Later, I knew It was a UTI and I needed to get a urinalysis to test, and amoxicillin to treat. I got my puppy to feel better with cranberry and d-mannose, but she most likely needed the vet visit for amoxicillin for the UTI bacterial infection. Dr Jungman listened to me and did the urine collection and sent it to the lab. The next day she called me with the results, that my puppy has a "significant" bacterial infection. She said she can do a more extensive test, but it runs at 250.00. She also suggested the same thing I choose, which was to do the two weeks of antibiotics and do a retest when she completes them. So I made the appointment and will do the urinalysis for 60.00. If the test results don't show improvement, then I may do the extensive testing; as the sample at the lab can be tested further.
Thank you Dr. Jungman for being on the level with people and caring about their pets.
~Zeppelyn's mom< /Review>

< review>
In March, my son's catalytic converter was stolen from his 2005 Toyota Prius while it was parked in the parking garage of his apartment complex on Finnian Way in Dublin.  We had it replaced by Minute Muffler and at our  request they welded it in place with rebar to make it more difficult to steal.
On the morning of July 14th my son started his Prius ( parked in the same parking garage) and heard the awful roar that indicated his catalytic converter  had been stolen again!  He saw the exhaust pipe hanging down and some wires dangling.  I called Minute Muffler and they were surprised because they had never heard of a catalytic converter being stolen after welding rebar in place.  We weren't sure the car was safe to drive because the exhaust pipe was hanging down so Scott offered to stop by the parking garage to check it out.  He came by after he closed on Wednesday and discovered The catalytic converter was still welded in place but the thieves had cut the pipe going into and out of the converter and tore out the wires to the O2 sensor. He thought it would be safe to drive and told us to follow him back to Minute Muffler and he would fix it.  He welded the pipes back in place and fixed the O2 sensor wires.  He not only did this after his closing time but refused payment for the repairs!
WE THANK SCOTT FOR GOING WAY ABOVE AND BEYOND- what amazing customer service!  WE HIGHLY RECOMMEND MINUTE MUFFLER!<//review>

The food is good. We ordered Garlic potatoes, Dip trio and stuffed green leaves for appetizers. The first 2 were good but the last one was bad. They also charge if you order pita for a second time with dip trio. For main course I ordered a Falafel wrap with french fries. <time>1570597366279<//time><Rate>4<//Rate><Review>A good place that this area was missing for quite some time. They offer good Mediterranean options and the whole experience is definitely above average in the area. Here's what I liked and what I did not like:
- Their customer service is great. The lady that runs the place will often come to your table to ask if everything is ok and bring you more water.
- They bring you complementary dips and pitta.
- They have special offers for USC students which are awesome in terms of quantity of food given the price.
- Their food quality is ok. I was never too impressed but it's not bad either.
- It's relatively pricier than most restaurants in the area but you also get what you pay for. It's a sit down restaurant. I moved to the neighborhood a few months ago, and have always wanted to try Amarena, as it is usually busy most days of the week. I put it off until my birthday last weekend, when i had my father and sister visiting from out of town. Everyone enjoyed their meals so much (I personally think I won with the wide pasta dish with prosciutto and sun-dried tomatoes), and the wine was delicious. My father and I were so pleased that we returned last night. We had a different waitress who, again, took care of us so well, providing wonderful suggestions for both eating and drinking. She managed to turn an ordinary Monday night into an unforgettable experience that I will never forget. At the end of the night, she even brought us some tiramisu which was amazing. A little slice of heaven.

It‚Äôs with great pleasure that I give you some highlights of what we ordered over our two dinners at Amarena, but I have to say, you cannot go wrong here:
1.) burrata- so creamy you might shed a little tear
2.) eggplant - how they managed to make this so savory and Smokey is beyond me. The sauce on this is might also make you shed a little tear.
3.) calamari- perfectly fried, wonderful dipping sauce. A simple classic that will not disappoint.
4.) chicken- crispy skin and juicy meat paired with expertly curated sides.
5.) pasta with sun-dried tomatoes- creamy, but light, balanced by crispy prosciutto pieces and tender sun-dried tomatoes.

First the food was not bad.  However, we had reservations here for Valentine's Dinner.  We had looked over the menu and felt good about this place.  Wasn't cheap, but wasn't $$$$$ either.  WELL, we feel ripped off like the other couples sitting near us.  First, NO MENU for this evening.  You had a choice of Steak, Fish or Vegetarian.  They did not show the price for dinner on the menu they gave us - or as a matter of fact - gave anyone else.  It included the appetizer, main course & dessert.  When we got the check we almost fainted.  The bill was for $85 per person + $3 for a can of Coke.  The service was not great.  They did give a long stem rose to each couple.  But, a $200 dinner where the food was not hot, we were hungry when we left, and we had not cocktails or wine.  This was a definite case of BAIT & SWITCH.  Even when we left we looked at the menu outside and nothing about the $85 per person for not great food.  If the meal was fabulous, then maybe, but it was slightly adequate.  IN GOOD FAITH, I CANNOT RECOMMEND THIS RESTAURANT OR IT'S STAFF!  I feel completely ripped off and I'm hungry and it hasn't been an hour since the meal.  Very disappointing!</Review>

Note: they no longer do happy hour Thursdays with free antipasta, which is what I was looking forward to, but the food here is ridiculously good. Let me start off by saying that I'm not an Italian fan because the food is typically so heavy and I don't care for Italian wine; BUT I am a believer when it comes to Amarena. Drinks weren't stellar (the sangria is weirdly spiced with cinnamon or something) and there aren't a lot of wine by the glass choices, but still the food made up for any of that nonsense.<//review>
